< Review>
Celebrated a very special milestone birthday of my partner's at this marvelous establishment, which honestly made the event that much better. Happy to have had been both recommended and invited to dine here by family who had raved about it. And for all the accolades given, Perle was not undersold in its excellence in attention to cuisine and wines.

Just East enough away from the bustle of San Francisco, and shy, below the beautiful wine valleys of California, Perle Wine Bar is nestled cozily on a quiet posh street in Oakland.

We dined one Thursday evening on the 25th of March 2021 to an a la-carte array befitting a tasting menu of much from what Perle has to offer.

Bravo to the chef and kitchen as well as to the front of house and service staff for such a marvelous meal and such a wonderful experience which will keep our memories of our little celebration reminiscing your restaurant in equal favour.< /Review>

<Review>My family has lived in Montclair for decades.  Now, we are blessed to have one of our favorite restaurants just a few minutes from home.  Perle provides fine dining quality food and style for an affordable price (entrees are around $30).

Chef Rob has a remarkable passion for food, which is evident in every bite you take and on full display with Perle's open kitchen.  Meanwhile, Chef Rob's co-owner, Marcus, runs the front of the house and serves as the sommelier.  His professionalism and hospitality match any fine dining establishment, but he has that unique ability to sincerely and genuinely treat every guest like family.

Go for the food because it is precise and deliberate.  Stay for the people because Rob and Marcus are great at what they do in the restaurant, but also the type of people you want as your neighbors, friends, and family!

ALL-STAR PEOPLE: Chef Rob and Marcus.< /Review>< user>

<userid>112152945953406766278< /userid>< user_name>
Lawrence Bair</user_name>
<Date>1521264339286< /Date><rate>4</rate>< Review>
Newbies in the neighborhood and just happened upon this place and it was a great experience.

We were headed for sushi next door but got rejected because we didn't have a reservation even though they had 6 empty tables.

Lucky for us!

Alex was at the door at Perle and was strait forward about our chances, but didn't rule out getting in for dinner. We killed some time and when we returned he went out of his way to shoehorn us in at the counter.

The place has that great classic bistro feel.. like you could be in any metropolitan city in the world.  Our stoolmates we're friendly and entertaining, the bartender was attentive and made us feel like we were dining with family.

Now the food....  Well for us it was fantastic! We're recent transplants from SF and we've dined in all sorts of restaurants all over the world and this place is at the top of our list.

We had a great bottle of pino recommended by their sommelier, the oysters with Thai dipping sauce, beef tartar with bone marrow and trout roe, and the biggest muscles I ever seen with spicey meatballs. What a great combination!

Every dish was plate licking good!

Highly recommend this place for a friendly & casual dining experience. You won't want to leave....</Review>

<userid>116147603313141834107< /userid><GmapID>0x808f879aaf0736d9:0x83c4e2a7e56b0ea1<//GmapID><Rating>3</Rating><time>1520703619384<//time>< review>
This new place looks great. It was crowded and VERY loud on a Friday night. Clientele much more Montclair than Oakland.

Menu is very edited, bistro-ish focused on oysters and caviar. Normally I am fine with a short menu but this was pretty repetitive so the choices were very limited. Prices are high. Good wine list with probably more than 15 wines by the glass.

Service was a little awkward, and we waited over 20' after our first course was cleared to get the second course.

Food was hit and miss. Green salad, well you don't expect too much, but most good places will do something interesting. This was pretty much just leaves on a plate, and the dressing was unevenly applied and all the pepper came in one bite. Mushroom soup was OK if very small-maybe 3 ounces? Oysters ironically were the low point; not delicious and too many things on top. Beef tartare with truffles and caviar was good.</review>

We went for Sunday Brunch with family and friends this afternoon and had a fantastic time! The menu is great... The decor is beautiful. The wine list is to.die.for. It's a well stocked, no joke wine list, at really fair prices. And we had some excellent cocktails. Is describe the fare as French with an American/California flair. Everything is very well thought out and cohesive.

We had Bloody Marys (yum); the cheese platter (double yum);  the mushroom cappuccino soup, which was warm and lovely, smelled as incredible as it tasted, and was presented beautifully; the eggs Benedict was divine - the best I've had in a very long time, with nice, crisp ham and perfect hollandaise; the avocado and smoked salmon toasts were light and beautiful and super tasty; and the burger was RIDICULOUSLY delicious, served with melty cheese and carmelized onions and a jus for dipping. My daughter ordered it, but I ended up eating about half of it because it was just that good.

The service was fast and friendly, and the ambience was comfortable and welcoming. Just thinking about the food is making me hungry! We'll definitely be going back to Perle for dinner, and putting it in our regular restaurant rotation.<//review>

<user_name>Amanda Bruyninckx</user_name><Resp>None</Resp><gmap_id>0x80dcb6c637a5987d:0x62685c37f8fb75d8</gmap_id><Text>***Top Ratings***
I've been to this Del Taco at least 50 times over the last year and the service has never disappointed. The manager (owner?) is almost always present, pleasent, and friendly.
The entire staff is attentive and polite.
Service is always quick and I don't think I have ever received my order incorrectly. The french fries may be hit or miss, but ingredients are fresh as is the Del promise.
The dining area is well maintained, cleaned, and stocked.   I have no complaints about this eatery and will stop in anytime I need a taco fix.
